###########################################################################################
####   This file contains the expressions of the 26 covariants generating
####   the ring of covariants of binary sextics.
####   The generic binary sextic is written without binimial coefficients:
####   f = a[0]*x^6+a[1]*x^5*y+a[2]*x^4*y^2+a[3]*x^3*y^3+a[4]*x^2*y^4+a[5]*x*y^5+a[6]*y^6
####   The 26 covariants are wriiten in the list LCov in the following order
####    [
####    [2, 0], [4, 0], [6, 0], [10, 0], [15, 0], 
####    [1, 6], 
####    [2, 4], [2, 8], 
####    [3, 2], [3, 6], [3, 8], [3, 12], 
####    [4, 4], [4, 6], [4, 10], 
####    [5, 2], [5, 4], [5, 8], 
####    [6, 6], [6,6], 
####    [7, 2], [7, 4], 
####    [8, 2], 
####    [9, 4], 
####    [10, 2], 
####    [12, 2]]  i.e. 
####    LCov[0] corresponds to C_{2,0}
####    LCov[1] corresponds to C_{4,0}
####    ...
####    LCov[25] corresponds to C_{12,2}
####    (in the notations of the note "Covariants of binary sextics").
###########################################################################################
